### [200] [BluTrain: A C++/CUDA Framework for AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24780)
*Adhitya Charan,Adwaid Suresh,Anuj Kumar,Aparna A,Dhanakumar K,Dharun M S,Dinesh G,Goutham Kumar Reddy K,Harshini V M,Jenifa D,Jona Delcy C A,Kathirvel S,Killi Uma Maheswara Rao,Kiruthik Kanna M,Kurra Vishnu Sai,Madhumithaa G K,Navin Kumar,Ram Charan Golla,Revathi T,Rishikkanth R,Sanjay Krishna M,Surendra Vendra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BluTrain是一个从零构建的轻量级通用深度学习训练框架，使用标准C++和核心CUDA编程模型实现。在8-GPU 6000 Ada系统上训练124M参数GPT-2（FP32）时，相比PyTorch实现了更高吞吐量（407K vs 395K tokens/s）和更低内存占用（减少22%），同时保持数值精度和收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模深度学习中的瓶颈已从模型架构转向系统工程——模型在训练中的吞吐量、内存占用和数值精度更多取决于架构在硬件上的表达方式，而非架构本身。现有框架在硬件表达控制和系统复杂性抽象之间存在矛盾，需要重复的编排逻辑。

Method: BluTrain从第一性原理出发，使用标准C++和核心CUDA编程模型构建。每层均原生实现：带反向模式自动微分的类型化张量模块、线性代数库、缓存分配器、多模式分布式执行模块以及基于MLIR的深度学习编译器。

Result: 在8-GPU 6000 Ada系统上训练124M参数GPT-2（FP32）的评估中，BluTrain达到平均407K tokens/s（vs PyTorch的395K），内存占用减少22%，保持数值保真度，收敛到略低的最终验证损失。

Conclusion: BluTrain通过原生硬件表达控制，在性能上超越行业基准。每一层都开放给原生调优，性能上限由框架自身决定。

Abstract: Progress in deep learning is, at scale, more a matter of systems engineering than of modelling: the behaviour of a model in training (its throughput, its memory footprint, and the numerical fidelity of the result) is determined less by the architecture itself than by how that architecture is expressed on the hardware. To achieve absolute control over this hardware expression while abstracting away systems complexity to make modelling seamless and eliminating the need for repetitive orchestration logic, BluTrain was architected from first principles as a robust, lightweight, and architecture-general training framework in standard C++ and the core CUDA programming model. Every layer is implemented natively: a typed tensor module with reverse-mode autograd, a linear-algebra library, a caching allocator, a multi-mode distributed-execution module, and an MLIR-based deep-learning compiler. In formal evaluations training a 124M-parameter GPT-2 baseline in FP32 on an 8-GPU 6000 Ada system, BluTrain outperforms industry-standard baselines in both throughput (sustaining an average of 407K tokens/s versus PyTorch's 395K tokens/s) and memory efficiency (achieving up to a 22% footprint reduction), while strictly preserving numerical fidelity and converging to a marginally lower final validation loss. With every layer explicitly open to native tuning, the performance ceiling is the framework's own to raise.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: While the field of Human Activity Recognition (HAR) continues to draw interest from researchers and advance in important ways, some key challenges remain. One of the most difficult aspects of building HAR models that show good performance in real-world settings is dealing with data diversity from device and sensor heterogeneity, and contextual changes that are intrinsic to real-world applications. While data diversity in HAR has been well-acknowledged in the literature, there remains a gap in understanding the effect of various types of distribution shifts on HAR models and the domain generalization problem that arises. Towards that end, this paper systematically evaluates 4 different types of distribution shifts, including variations in device type, sensor placement, sampling rate, and user behavior. Quantifying their effects, we illustrate that diversity shifts predominantly define all types of shifts, indicating the existence of unique features that are not shared across different domains. We then introduce a uniform HAR-based distribution shift benchmarks and conduct a comprehensive evaluation of up to 28 domain generalization methods. Our analysis exposes the limitations of current domain generalization algorithms in achieving model generalizability, marginally outperforming the empirical risk minimization baseline. This work represents the first systematic exploration of domain generalization and adaptation concerning specific distribution shifts in sensor-based HAR, offering an open-source benchmark platform and datasets to spur further research.

Motivation: 混沌动力学的逆问题（从最终状态推断初始条件）由于病态性、非唯一性、不稳定性以及混沌时间反演动力学而长期未得到有效解决。

Method: 提出双向条件流匹配（Bi-CFM），学习初始状态与最终状态分布之间的双向映射，捕获混沌演化的随机性并缓解指数级误差累积；针对具有守恒律的系统，进一步提出守恒约束的CBi-CFM。

Result: 在Lorenz、Circuit和高维Lorenz 96系统上，Bi-CFM在五项分布级指标上优于基线，同时实现超两个数量级的加速；在三体行星散射问题中，CBi-CFM的守恒误差与真实值相当；在真实球状星团观测数据上，方法取得了精度上的进步。

Conclusion: 该方法为长时标真实世界混沌动力学的逆问题提供了一条可扩展的有效路径。

Abstract: Modeling chaotic systems is crucial yet challenging. Inverse problems in chaotic dynamics, namely inferring initial conditions from final states, remain largely unsolved because of ill-posedness, non-uniqueness, instability, and potentially chaotic time-reverse dynamics. We address this open problem with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching (Bi-CFM), which learns bidirectional mappings between distributions of initial and final states to capture the stochasticity of chaotic evolution and mitigate exponential error accumulation over time. Furthermore, for systems with conservation laws, we extend it to Conservation-constrained Bi-CFM (CBi-CFM). Across the classic Lorenz, Circuit, and high-dimensional Lorenz 96 systems, Bi-CFM improves five distribution-level metrics over baselines while achieving a speedup of more than two orders of magnitude. In the three-body planet-planet scattering problem in planetary dynamics, CBi-CFM better respects conservation laws, with conservation errors comparable to those of the ground truth. Finally, on real observations of globular clusters, collisional million-body systems shaped by $\sim 10^{10}$ years (10 Gyr) of evolution, our method represents an advance in accuracy, establishing a scalable route to solving inverse problems of long-timescale real-world chaotic dynamics.

</details>


### [203] [Difference-Making without Making a Difference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24832)
*Sander Beckers*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Andreas & Günther提出的七种实际因果定义实际可归为三类（事实差异制造、反事实差异制造、规则性基础），并证明其最新定义同时包含这三类，说明这些分类是虚假的区分。进一步比较发现，这削弱了他们所有的七个理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 批评和挑战Andreas & Günther关于实际因果的七种定义及其分类体系，指出其分类标准的混淆和内部不一致性。

Method: 通过逻辑分析和关键案例比较，证明Andreas & Günther最新的事实差异制造定义同时包含了三种因果类型，并通过案例检验揭示所有七个定义的缺陷。

Result: 证明了Andreas & Günther的三种分类（事实差异制造、反事实差异制造、规则性基础）是虚假区分，且他们的七个定义都存在根本性问题。

Conclusion: Andreas & Günther的七种实际因果定义分类体系存在内部矛盾，其最新定义混合了三种类型，表明这些分类"没有区别的区别"，从而削弱了整个理论框架的有效性。

Abstract: Over a series of seven papers, Andreas & Günther have introduced seven definitions of actual causation and have classified them as belonging to three different, competing, types of accounts: factual difference-making, counterfactual difference-making, and regularity-based. I show that their most recent - factual difference-making - definition instantiates all three types, thereby proving that these are distinctions without a difference. I further compare their novel account to the other six accounts on several crucial examples, revealing that this undermines all seven of their accounts.

</details>


### [204] [Accuracy and Satisfaction in Multi-Turn LLM Dialogues for NFR Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24834)
*Ali Pourghasemi Fatideh,Wilder Baldwin,Maria Dhakal,Collin McMillan,Sepideh Ghanavati*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了开发者与LLM对话助手（GitHub Copilot）在评估非功能需求（NFRs）时的多轮对话准确性与质量。通过49名程序员对148个HIPAA合规相关的NFRs进行评估，发现开发者倾向于认同LLM的评估，但准确性较低；系统响应过长和信息过多会降低用户满意度，而主动交互则能提升满意度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估基准仅关注功能正确性，忽略了非功能需求（NFRs）评估中对话质量与准确性的关键缺口。NFRs具有模糊性、上下文依赖性和跨程序模块等特点，需要超越单轮准确性的多轮交互评估方法。

Method: 招募49名程序员使用GitHub Copilot对iTrust代码库中148个HIPAA衍生的NFRs进行多轮对话评估，从需求满足程度、推理和代码定位三个维度衡量，并建模用户满意度。

Result: 开发者倾向于同意LLM的评估结果，但与专家标注的真实标签相比准确率较低。较长的系统响应和更多提供信息的轮次会负面影响用户满意度，而主动交互行为则对满意度有正向影响。

Conclusion: 为设计支持NFR评估的LLM对话系统提供了洞见，强调系统应注重交互质量而非单纯增加信息量，并需考虑主动交互策略以提升用户体验。

Abstract: LLM-based dialogue assistants have become mainstream tools for software developers, yet current evaluation benchmarks focus exclusively on functional correctness. This leaves a critical gap in assessing the quality and accuracy of these conversations when handling Non-Functional Requirements (NFRs), which are inherently vague, context-dependent, and involve many parts of a program. Evaluating how well these systems support collaborative reasoning about NFRs requires methods that go beyond single-turn accuracy to capture both the correctness of the system's outputs and the quality of the multi-turn interaction. In this paper, we investigate the accuracy and quality of multi-turn conversations between developers and an LLM-based agent in the domain of Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) regulatory compliance. We hired 49 programmers to interact with GitHub Copilot to assess 148 HIPAA-derived NFRs against the iTrust codebase, a system designed to comply with HIPAA regulations, across three dimensions: requirement satisfaction level, reasoning, and code localization. We find that developers tend to agree with LLM assessments, but accuracy against expert ground truth is low. We model user satisfaction and find that longer system responses and more information-providing turns negatively affect user satisfaction, whereas proactive interactions positively affect it. Our findings provide insights for designing LLM-based dialogue systems that support NFR assessment.

### [205] [Grading the Grader: Lessons from Evaluating an Agentic Data Analysis System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24839)
*Tian Zheng,Kai-Tai Hsu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三层人机协同分级评估级联架构（严格正则匹配→宽松LLM评估→片段人工审查），用于评估智能体数据分析系统LAMBDA在153个QRData任务上的输出。宽松评估器的精确率达100%、召回率97%；关键词锚定提取将严格评估器召回率提升60个百分点；迭代提示机制将评估运行成功率从36%提升至97%，且发现原始问题重新注入无益，提示实质是答案模板线索。变量类型是与评估流水线动态最相关的任务元数据字段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体数据分析系统产生包含代码、数值结果和语言诊断的丰富输出，其评估比单轮LLM响应更具挑战性，需要区分智能体输出与真实答案之间的真正分歧与评分伪影。现有评估方法缺乏对这种多模态输出的可靠分级策略研究。

Method: 在DSGym的153个QRData数值任务上应用多智能体数据分析系统LAMBDA，开发并评估三层人机评估级联：严格正则匹配、基于LLM的宽松评估、基于片段的人工审查。采用关键词锚定提取、迭代提示（nudge）机制等技术，评估不同策略对分级质量的影响。

Result: 两种自动评估器均达到100%观测精确率（0/70假阳性）；宽松评估器召回率97%；关键词锚定提取将严格评估器召回率较末位数字启发式提升60个百分点；迭代提示将运行成功率从36%提升至97%，宽松通过率从16%提升至46%；原始问题重新注入未见益处；变量类型是与评估流水线动态最相关的元数据字段。

Conclusion: 提出的三层级联评估框架有效提升了智能体数据分析系统的评估可靠性，揭示了不同分级策略的互补失败模式，并指出变量类型是关键影响因素。

Abstract: Agentic data analysis systems produce rich outputs, including code, numerical results, and verbal diagnostics. This makes them more challenging to evaluate than single-turn LLM responses. It is therefore necessary to distinguish genuine disagreement between an agent's output and a ground-truth answer from grading artifacts. We investigate how reliably automated graders assess such a system and what strategies improve grading quality by applying LAMBDA, a multi-agent data-analysis system, on 153 numerical QRData tasks from DSGym. We develop and evaluate a three-layer human-AI grading cascade: strict regex matching, LLM-based lenient grading, and snippet-based human inspection, which combines non-GenAI and GenAI strategies with different failure profiles. Both automated graders achieve 100% observed precision (0/70 false positives). The lenient grader's recall is 97% against human labels. A keyword-anchored extraction pipeline raises the strict grader's recall by 60 percentage points over a last-number heuristic; the lenient grader is architecturally parser-independent. An iterative nudge mechanism raises grading run success from 36% to 97% and lenient-pass rates from 16% to 46%; comparing nudging with and without original-question re-injection shows that re-injection offers no benefit, confirming the nudge as an answer template cue. We further observe in this case study that variable type is the task metadata field most consistently associated with grading pipeline dynamics and observed outcome grades.

</details>


### [206] [Matching Tasks to Objectives: Fine-Tuning and Prompt-Tuning Strategies for Encoder-Decoder Pre-trained Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24841)
*Ahmad Pouramini,Hesham Faili*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Match Task to Objective (MTO)框架，通过匹配预训练目标与下游任务目标，结合多目标预训练和适应性微调模板，在少样本和全数据集场景下显著提升编码器-解码器语言模型在生成和问答任务上的性能，性能提升超120%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同预训练目标对编码器-解码器语言模型在生成和问答任务中性能的影响，尤其是在常识知识检索与补全方面，并寻求自动化匹配任务与最优预训练目标的方法。

Method: 提出MTO框架：1) 自动确定给定任务对应最合适的预训练目标；2) 基于识别出的目标，通过无监督训练自动准备任务相关数据进行适应；3) 设计与新目标对齐的模板用于微调；4) 将方法扩展到prompt-tuning中，优化软提示工程。

Result: 在少样本设置下，相比传统方法性能提升超过120%；显著优于相关少样本工作；在全数据集场景下也超越基线；同时有效提升了prompt-tuning性能。

Conclusion: 多目标对齐策略能精准指导特定任务下模型的选择与优化，具有重要的实用价值。

Abstract: Prompt-based learning has emerged as a dominant paradigm in natural language processing. This study explores the impact of diverse pre-training objectives on the performance of encoder-decoder pre-trained language models across generation and question answering tasks, with a focus on commonsense knowledge retrieval and completion. We highlight the benefits of incorporating multiple objectives during both pre-training and fine-tuning stages. We introduce the Match Task to Objective (MTO) framework and methods for determining the appropriate objective for a given task. This framework offers automated methods to prepare task-related data for adaptation through unsupervised training, based on the identified objective. In the fine-tuning stage, we design novel templates that align with the objectives of the pre-training and adaptation stages. When aligned with task requirements, these strategies can achieve a performance gain of over 120\% compared to conventional methods in few-shot settings. They significantly outperform related works in few-shot settings and exceed the baseline even in full-dataset scenarios. Furthermore, we extend this approach to include prompt-tuning methodologies, providing guidance for more effective soft prompt engineering and optimization. Our strategies significantly enhance prompt-tuning performance as well. These insights hold substantial value, precisely guiding the selection and optimization of models customized for specific tasks. Code is available at https://github.com/puraminy/MTO/

### [207] [World Models in Pieces: Structural Certification for General Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24842)
*Yikai Lu,Yifei Wu,Xinyu Lu,Tongxin Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出结构认证框架，通过将通用智能体的能力分解到局部世界模型中，实现可部署的可靠性保证，并证明该框架在误差界上具有紧致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大世界场景下，智能体无法具备通用能力，其能力必然在世界模型的不同片段中专门化。标准的一致性保证无法区分关键瓶颈与无关失败，导致最坏情况分析失去信息量。

Method: 首先形式化证明了通用智能体并非真正通用，使得标准最坏情况分析失效。然后提出结构认证——一种基于转移局部的框架，将有界目标条件性能映射到智能体内部世界模型的逐条目保证。通过深度组合目标过滤特定转移，并证明通用智能体在这些目标上具有结构化的世界模型，误差界为O(1/n)+O(δ)。

Result: 该误差界在小δ区域是紧的，且结构认证明确保证了该区域的存在性。这使得能够定位长程规划可靠的特定转移，从而实现通用智能体的可认证部署。

Conclusion: 结构认证框架通过局部化关键转移，解决了大世界场景下通用智能体无法普遍适用的根本问题，为可认证部署提供了理论保证。

Abstract: In the big-world regime, agents cannot be universally capable and their ability is inevitably specialized across a world model in pieces. Consequently, standard uniform guarantees fail to distinguish between the understanding of critical bottlenecks and irrelevant failures. We first formalize this limitation by proving that general agents are not universal, rendering standard worst-case analysis uninformative. To overcome this, we introduce structural certification, a transition-local framework that maps bounded goal-conditioned performance to entry-wise guarantees on the agent's internal world model. Our main contribution is constructive. We provide algorithms that filter specific transitions using deep compositional goals and prove that a general agent on these goals has a structural world model with a $\mathcal{O}(1/n) + \mathcal{O}(δ)$ error bound. Conversely, this bound is tight in the small-$δ$ regime, whose existence is explicitly guaranteed by our certification. These results enable the certifiable deployment of general agents by localizing the specific transitions where long-horizon planning is reliable.

</details>


### [208] [OpenThoughts-Agent: Data Recipes for Agentic Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24855)
*Negin Raoof,Richard Zhuang,Marianna Nezhurina,Etash Guha,Atula Tejaswi,Ryan Marten,Charlie F. Ruan,Tyler Griggs,Alexander Glenn Shaw,Hritik Bansal,E. Kelly Buchanan,Artem Gazizov,Reinhard Heckel,Chinmay Hegde,Sankalp Jajee,Daanish Khazi,Emmanouil Koukoumidis,Xiangyi Li,Hange Liu,Shlok Natarajan,Harsh Raj,Nicholas Roberts,Ethan Shen,Nishad Singhi,Michael Siu,Ashima Suvarna,Hanwen Xing,Patrick Yubeaton,Robert Zhang,Leon Liangyu Chen,Xiaokun Chen,Steven Dillmann,Saadia Gabriel,Xunyi Jiang,Anurag Kashyap,Boxuan Li,Yein Park,Minh Pham,Sujay Sanghavi,Lin Shi,Ke Sun,Yixin Wang,Zhiwei Xu,Erica Zhang,Siyan Zhao,Wanjia Zhao,Jenia Jitsev,Alex Dimakis,Benjamin Feuer,Ludwig Schmidt*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了OpenThoughts-Agent (OT-Agent)项目，构建了完全开放的数据筛选流程用于训练智能体模型。通过100+控制消融实验系统研究流程各阶段，筛选出10万条训练数据微调Qwen3-32B，在7个智能体基准上平均准确率44.8%，比最强现有开源模型(Nemotron-Terminal-32B, 40.9%)提升3.9个百分点，且训练数据展现强扩展性。所有数据、流程、模型均已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源智能体模型(如SWE-Smith, SERA, Nemotron-Terminal)通常只针对单一基准进行训练，缺乏能够跨多样智能体任务泛化的训练数据和方法，因此亟需探索如何筛选训练数据以培养广泛能力的智能体模型。

Method: 构建完全开放的数据筛选流程，通过100+控制消融实验系统研究流程各阶段(任务来源、多样性等)的影响，最终筛选出10万条训练数据用于微调Qwen3-32B。

Result: 微调后的Qwen3-32B在7个智能体基准上平均准确率44.8%，比最强现有开源模型Nemotron-Terminal-32B(40.9%)提升3.9个百分点；训练数据在计算控制条件下，各训练集规模均优于其他开源数据集，展现强扩展性。

Conclusion: 开放的OT-Agent数据筛选流程有效提升了智能体模型的跨任务泛化能力，证明了任务来源和多样性的重要性，为智能体模型训练提供了可复现的开源方案。

Abstract: Agentic language models dramatically expand the applications of AI yet little is publicly known about how to curate training data for broadly capable agents. Existing open efforts such as SWE-Smith, SERA, and Nemotron-Terminal typically target a single benchmark, leaving open the question of how to train models that generalize across diverse agentic tasks. The OpenThoughts-Agent (OT-Agent) project addresses this gap with a fully open data curation pipeline for training agentic models. We conduct more than 100 controlled ablation experiments to systematically investigate each stage of the pipeline, yielding insights on the importance of task sources and diversity. We then assemble a training set of 100K examples from our pipeline and fine-tune Qwen3-32B on this dataset, which yields an average accuracy of 44.8% across seven agentic benchmarks and a 3.9 percentage point improvement over the strongest existing open data agentic model (Nemotron-Terminal-32B, 40.9%). Moreover, our training data exhibits strong scaling properties, outperforming alternative open datasets at every training set size in compute-controlled comparisons. We publicly release our training sets, data pipeline, experimental data, and models at openthoughts.ai to support future open research on agentic model training.

</details>

### [209] [PCB-QA: Evaluating LLMs over the First Printed Circuit Board Design Question-Answer Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23704)
*Sahana Srinivasan,Benjamin Tan,Benjamin Turnbull,Hammond Pearce*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出PCB-QA数据集（包含480个PCB问答对，覆盖8个开源硬件项目），并评估了4个LLM在理解PCB设计文件方面的能力。研究发现，使用JSON文本格式时，Gemini 3 Flash Preview的准确率达到93%，表明文本化PCB设计格式可被LLM有效处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在集成电路EDA领域已展现能力，但在PCB设计与分析任务中的应用尚待探索，主要原因在于：(1)缺乏文本形式的PCB数据集来评估LLM；(2)缺乏指导LLM处理不同类型PCB设计文件的提示方法。

Method: 创建PCB-QA数据集：从8个不同复杂度的开源硬件项目中手工构建480个问答对，涵盖组件连接、数据手册检查和SPICE仿真数据等多方面。以该数据集为基准，用不同表示形式（PDF图形、KiCAD文件、JSON文本等）提示LLM并记录结果，评估4个SOTA LLM。

Result: Gemini 3 Flash Preview在使用所提出的JSON文本格式时达到93%的准确率，表明文本化PCB设计格式能被LLM有效评估。

Conclusion: 该开放数据集是推动LLM集成到PCB设计生命周期中的第一步，证明LLM能够理解文本形式的PCB设计文件。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated capabilities in electronic design automation (EDA) for integrated circuits. However, their applications in printed circuit board (PCB) design and analysis tasks remain underexplored. In part, this is due to a (1) a lack of text-based PCB datasets to evaluate LLMs and (2) a lack of methodologies for prompting LLMs with different types of PCB design files. To address this gap, our paper proposes PCB-QA: a manually created questionnaire dataset amounting to 480 question-answer pairs for PCBs, derived from 8 different open-source hardware projects of varying complexities. We examine multiple aspects of PCB designs and cover questions about component connections, datasheet examination, and simulation data obtainable via SPICE. Using our dataset as a benchmark, we prompt LLMs with different representations (and combinations) of PCB design files and record observations. This allows us to measure, for the first time, if LLMs can understand schematics and netlists in their "native forms" (i.e. graphical PDFs, KiCAD-format design files) or if textual formats are preferred. Including both commercial and open-weight models, we benchmark 4 state-of-the-art LLMs on our dataset, finding that Gemini 3 Flash Preview can answer questions with an accuracy of 93% using a proposed JSON-based textual format. This demonstrates that text-based PCB design formats can be evaluated by LLMs. Our open-source questionnaire is the first step towards enabling LLM integrations within the PCB design life cycle.

### [210] [VeriPilot: An LLM-Powered Verilog Debugging Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23759)
*Yihan Wang,Cheng Liu,Jiazheng Zhang,Lei Zhang,Long Cheng,Xiaowei Li,Huawei Li*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: VeriPilot是一个利用黄金参考模型进行细粒度Verilog调试的LLM框架，通过信号级语义对齐和CDFG引导的逐步追踪，将GPT-4o的修复成功率从54.3%提升至85.71%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的Verilog调试方法仅依赖测试输出和编译器反馈进行端到端修复，难以处理根因与输出相距较远的复杂bug，尤其在大型代码库中长上下文进一步限制了推理效率。

Method: VeriPilot利用黄金参考模型，通过LLM分析对齐Verilog设计与黄金模型之间的内部变量语义，然后基于静态分析提取的控制-数据流图(CDFG)进行逐步信号追踪，定位最小可疑代码区域并从黄金模型中提取对应的正确实现，最后将这些结构化信息提供给LLM进行推理和自动代码修复。

Result: 在NVIDIA的CVDP基准测试上，VeriPilot将GPT-4o的修复成功率从54.3%提升至85.71%，显著提高了复杂Verilog设计的bug定位准确性和修复效果。

Conclusion: VeriPilot证明了利用黄金参考模型进行细粒度信号级语义对齐和结构化CDFG追踪能有效突破端到端LLM调试方法在复杂bug上的性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Verilog debugging remains one of the most time-consuming stages in digital circuit design. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled automated debugging; however, most existing approaches rely solely on test outputs and compiler feedback in an end-to-end manner, limiting their effectiveness on complex bugs. A key challenge is that the root cause of an error may be far removed from its observable outputs, making it difficult for LLMs to trace long dependency chains in code. This challenge is further exacerbated in large codebases, where long context lengths hinder efficient reasoning. To address these limitations, we propose VeriPilot, an LLM-powered debugging framework that leverages golden reference models to enable fine-grained bug localization and repair. VeriPilot goes beyond output-level comparison by aligning internal variable semantics between the Verilog design and its corresponding golden model through LLM-based analysis. It then performs step-by-step signal tracing using Control-Data-Flow Graphs (CDFGs) derived from static analysis, identifying a minimal set of suspicious code regions along with their correct counterparts from the golden model. These structured insights are subsequently provided to the LLM to guide reasoning and automated code repair. Experimental results on the Comprehensive Verilog Design Problems (CVDP) benchmark from NVIDIA demonstrate that VeriPilot improves the repair success rate of GPT-4o from 54.3\% to 85.71\%, significantly enhancing both bug localization accuracy and repair effectiveness for complex Verilog designs. The source code and benchmark are publicly available at Github https://github.com/YihanWn/VeriPilot.git.

</details>


<div id='cs.PF'></div>

# cs.PF [[Back]](#toc)

### [211] [LMS-AR: LMS Prediction-based Adaptive Regulator for Memory Bandwidth in Multicore Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23945)
*Sudarshan Srinivasan,Deepak Gangadharan,Dip Goswami*

Main category: cs.PF

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于LMS预测的自适应内存带宽调节机制LMS-AR，通过在主核上部署监测与调节模块，利用自适应滤波预测各核心带宽需求，有效缓解多核系统的内存带宽竞争，相比Memguard显著降低了性能下降比率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多核系统中内存带宽竞争严重影响应用性能和服务质量（QoS）保障，需要有效的内存带宽调节机制来降低性能不确定性，提升多核系统的可信赖性。

Method: 在Linux内核模块中实现LMS-AR（LMS Prediction-based Adaptive Regulator），采用主核从外部进行监测和调节（非专用控制器），利用自适应滤波技术预测每核心的带宽需求，并将计算密集型算法部署在非受控核心上以避免干扰。

Result: 使用SPEC CPU 2017基准测试在多核心上实验，相比Memguard，该方法在内存竞争导致的性能下降比率上有显著改善。

Conclusion: LMS-AR通过主核外挂监测与调节、自适应预测带宽需求的方式，有效缓解内存带宽竞争，提升了多核系统的性能稳定性和资源可管理性。

Abstract: Memory bandwidth contention in multi-core systems severely impacts application performance and quality-of-service (QoS) guarantees. Regulating the shared memory bandwidth mitigates the memory performance uncertainty thereby making it a manageable resource and improving trustworthiness of multi-core systems. In this work we propose a memory bandwidth regulation mechanism LMS-AR, i.e., LMS Prediction-based Adaptive Regulator within a Linux kernel module to distribute the memory bandwidth as a resource among the CPU cores. We describe a design in which both monitoring and regulation is enforced from outside by a master core - which is not a dedicated controller for regulation. This allows for plugging in computationally heavy prediction and regulation algorithms without interfering with the regulated core. An adaptive filtering technique was employed for prediction of per-core bandwidth requirement. We conducted several experiments with SPEC CPU 2017 benchmarks distributed across multiple cores. Our proposed approach demonstrated significant improvement over Memguard with respect to slowdown ratios caused due to memory contention. Our solution is hosted publicly at $\href{https://github.com/ss22ongithub/LMSAdaptiveRegulator}{https://github.com/ss22ongithub/LMSAdaptiveRegulator}$.

</details>
